</div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEioZWW9K6bruf7af1vCre8s471Bs_NK_Q_m_vJsPsKoVchfyZZaEid-GekGd4Yce3Joa8pMRI1g3Dcrs7ueyK6jHYRtLzuh34AzB41TX73uj5vznD_QjwQ2If5QMGhW7FgysEMR5SSFSVs/s1600/05.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="470" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEioZWW9K6bruf7af1vCre8s471Bs_NK_Q_m_vJsPsKoVchfyZZaEid-GekGd4Yce3Joa8pMRI1g3Dcrs7ueyK6jHYRtLzuh34AzB41TX73uj5vznD_QjwQ2If5QMGhW7FgysEMR5SSFSVs/s640/05.jpg" width="640" /></a></div><div style="text-align: center;"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><b>Foto 06 &#8211;</b> Senhoras e crianças prestigiam evento da Polícia nos anos 70:</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><br />
</div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjJwJR74C4_nDF59om6ihVFS8Jdle5W4Bq53r-ML09_0VHa5dqYpeghle_4w9JoDe94a5CItmaqsh6jigWpvTD0wNqHkTDFeSZnwA_U2r3jjvUGzsPGtGl38imdU1m40qoNA-luK1lt81I/s1600/06.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="480" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjJwJR74C4_nDF59om6ihVFS8Jdle5W4Bq53r-ML09_0VHa5dqYpeghle_4w9JoDe94a5CItmaqsh6jigWpvTD0wNqHkTDFeSZnwA_U2r3jjvUGzsPGtGl38imdU1m40qoNA-luK1lt81I/s640/06.jpg" width="640" /></a></div><div style="text-align: center;"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: justify;"></div><div style="text-align: justify;"></div><div style="text-align: justify;"></div><div style="text-align: justify;"><b>Foto 07 &#8211;</b> Pose do Coronel Marcílio Pio Chaves em foto dos anos 70:</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: justify;"></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjtitGBZdKbpXgzFyqfV6-59QD5utZm6nkJ_nT0gjPG9_erwlOu3bEoQ96Ltp_pGQC1YiYzLJlRKG7vViM3V30JVL7I4DHZEbhJ3ZoXGfPuqOfTEv2ibST38KWRE4mPyQCfH5MgyvSL4tA/s1600/07.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="482" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjtitGBZdKbpXgzFyqfV6-59QD5utZm6nkJ_nT0gjPG9_erwlOu3bEoQ96Ltp_pGQC1YiYzLJlRKG7vViM3V30JVL7I4DHZEbhJ3ZoXGfPuqOfTEv2ibST38KWRE4mPyQCfH5MgyvSL4tA/s640/07.jpg" width="640" /></a></div><div style="text-align: center;"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><b>Foto 08 &#8211; </b>Policial cumprimenta criança durante evento nos anos 80:</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: justify;"></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEheK_Qdo-SFoOMA-0PheSD0yeUQRCuQu3vOmDLMFPK5gajK1CdzofwZbeH_yFB50vSQCxfvNRrfK20Oi7MFnyq-lCwqnOfpPRg0oIUY0oY9cqNoNXx6fZUwQMi5bhMArQPWleTVlkOZ-rc/s1600/08.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEheK_Qdo-SFoOMA-0PheSD0yeUQRCuQu3vOmDLMFPK5gajK1CdzofwZbeH_yFB50vSQCxfvNRrfK20Oi7MFnyq-lCwqnOfpPRg0oIUY0oY9cqNoNXx6fZUwQMi5bhMArQPWleTVlkOZ-rc/s640/08.jpg" width="452" /></a></div><div style="text-align: center;"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><b>Foto 09 &#8211; </b>Mais uma criança sendo cumprimentada (Anos 80):</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: justify;"></div><div style="text-align: justify;"></div><div style="text-align: justify;"></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjzm8sR8Or7mLKfGO1Fu3g6VnOCC1NkateMhFOM3vNbspTbv-YGi-YvtJEiS15v5cw-okBdfbyflP-W1UB5QHcLZqR6lQnnikaol_ZyxQJbSWcQCOjW9BdPQDobSCA2-hVlW-osOo8934Y/s1600/09.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjzm8sR8Or7mLKfGO1Fu3g6VnOCC1NkateMhFOM3vNbspTbv-YGi-YvtJEiS15v5cw-okBdfbyflP-W1UB5QHcLZqR6lQnnikaol_ZyxQJbSWcQCOjW9BdPQDobSCA2-hVlW-osOo8934Y/s640/09.jpg" width="442" /></a></div><div style="text-align: center;"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><b>Foto 10 &#8211; </b>Criança batendo continência durante evento nos anos 80:</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: justify;"></div><div style="text-align: justify;"></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEiswESGZxrIYBx9lXpeKfVLPnDDTv5Gd0dOilu7wawfhlUY2tFDEa811YSLtzq-SdiJLNGXO0t8Y-ZiNNFC3Y_JzrwxtXas5457WWeZI9YZGkEhaZZ0pL5uk0QX7CccfehBi59FHRtOcys/s1600/10.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEiswESGZxrIYBx9lXpeKfVLPnDDTv5Gd0dOilu7wawfhlUY2tFDEa811YSLtzq-SdiJLNGXO0t8Y-ZiNNFC3Y_JzrwxtXas5457WWeZI9YZGkEhaZZ0pL5uk0QX7CccfehBi59FHRtOcys/s640/10.jpg" width="444" /></a></div><div style="text-align: center;"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><b>Foto 11 &#8211; </b>Crianças participam de evento da polícia militar nos anos 80:</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><br />
</div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEifMh7Mg_BSEYHnW1urB2eLBj0mpW7sRfMD4CC4wIktUtpOTHuoGrvOqB91ZiFdwWdb8V0nd4rNB1cCfznIOizpUAZszhWcUEjgaLY-6IS5Y07kwl-ifsC2tgJHR5iU0q6UpPRZJG2z1Ag/s1600/11.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="446" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEifMh7Mg_BSEYHnW1urB2eLBj0mpW7sRfMD4CC4wIktUtpOTHuoGrvOqB91ZiFdwWdb8V0nd4rNB1cCfznIOizpUAZszhWcUEjgaLY-6IS5Y07kwl-ifsC2tgJHR5iU0q6UpPRZJG2z1Ag/s640/11.jpg" width="640" /></a></div><div style="text-align: center;"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><b>Foto 12 &#8211;</b> Mais uma imagem das crianças dentro do Batalhão. Destaque para o ex-prefeito de Campina Grande, Antônio Carvalho, ao fundo (Anos 80):</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: justify;"></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjS8E4aq1Ku5c6_E2Mji7avsoJapXnTAZ4Jpa_nz9yIR3lhdeQ2nTCbjSv6Mty19P3uQsmzvmCYyX7HtPxAaWd8uXW_Dua2jtdhBuKtrEEHzjjeYg2o-mcfcPDuacjJRG3HUBiLXampGuE/s1600/12.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="422" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjS8E4aq1Ku5c6_E2Mji7avsoJapXnTAZ4Jpa_nz9yIR3lhdeQ2nTCbjSv6Mty19P3uQsmzvmCYyX7HtPxAaWd8uXW_Dua2jtdhBuKtrEEHzjjeYg2o-mcfcPDuacjJRG3HUBiLXampGuE/s640/12.jpg" width="640" /></a></div><div style="text-align: center;"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><b>Foto 13 &#8211;</b> Desfile da Polícia Militar durante os anos 80:</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: justify;"></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEiH7BvY6oPa-rZrnqIA0jY-oZrkSGOg9Bzxna-5GrhFHW8azwWowCPrME0qE36fFnclp9nGgBDqTI3zng5cb5B2Pi9UZSus1Bvq_TZM-Knl_inl_KLKfa_-diPhdhMWI65GiUFfv61d-6A/s1600/13.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="426" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEiH7BvY6oPa-rZrnqIA0jY-oZrkSGOg9Bzxna-5GrhFHW8azwWowCPrME0qE36fFnclp9nGgBDqTI3zng5cb5B2Pi9UZSus1Bvq_TZM-Knl_inl_KLKfa_-diPhdhMWI65GiUFfv61d-6A/s640/13.jpg" width="640" /></a></div><div style="text-align: center;"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><b>Foto 14 &#8211;</b> Oficiais passam em revista de tropas, em frente a Pediatria do Hospital Pedro I (Anos 80):</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: justify;"></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhPr-IGwvJk1Qa_9bblVsJfn1GGDHFzotWSBLqk6e5cFJWylhKxlda7oI42OArUaz61AcwGrOwmaelOgoX3JriGgVxrmwiArjJ6elo_ZQm9IhX6Qm7YETxLNLC78b1VephQ76MXdyXdUm0/s1600/14.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="420" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhPr-IGwvJk1Qa_9bblVsJfn1GGDHFzotWSBLqk6e5cFJWylhKxlda7oI42OArUaz61AcwGrOwmaelOgoX3JriGgVxrmwiArjJ6elo_ZQm9IhX6Qm7YETxLNLC78b1VephQ76MXdyXdUm0/s640/14.jpg" width="640" /></a></div><div style="text-align: center;"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><b>Foto 15 &#8211; </b>Desfile da Polícia Militar realizado em outro em 1983:</div><div style="text-align: justify;"><br />
</div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhywWE3IEBV4GmhozZrLnAb7Td507azzc6Mov0sasbIWdrcy2pkuKG5dpEiXlwnTclvPY8cuXwK02_U_8DO7JjXFIJYUZn4SlOFaVG-FYKbxKABGbR2oDfB6Emd60c27tKIGX-WgB7VTQA/s1600/15.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="436" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhywWE3IEBV4GmhozZrLnAb7Td507azzc6Mov0sasbIWdrcy2pkuKG5dpEiXlwnTclvPY8cuXwK02_U_8DO7JjXFIJYUZn4SlOFaVG-FYKbxKABGbR2oDfB6Emd60c27tKIGX-WgB7VTQA/s640/15.jpg" width="640" /></a></div><div style="text-align: center;"><br />
</div><div style="text-align: justify;">Nos próximos dias, a sexta parte do especial, aguardem.</div>

<h2 class='title'>Colabore Conosco!</h2>
<div class='widget-content'>
A História é Feita de Registros e Memórias!<br/>Colabore com nosso resgate nos enviando fotos, áudios, vídeos, etc... Fatos que remetam ao pretérito campinense.<br/>Teremos prazer em citar quem nos enviar.<br/><span style="font-weight: bold;">(retalhoscg@hotmail.com)</span><br/>
</div>
